<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/West_Frisian_language" class="extiw" title="w:West Frisian language">West Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fy"><a href = vnd.unilang:sjouwen.html>sjouwe</a></i>, believed to be from <i class="Latn mention" lang="ofs">*ski≈çua</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="ofs">*skiƒÅva</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">‚Äú</span><span class="mention-gloss">to slide, shove</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">‚Äù</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, a variant of <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Frisian" class="extiw" title="w:Old Frisian">Old Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="ofs">sk≈´va</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">‚Äú</span><span class="mention-gloss">to push, shove</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">‚Äù</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*skeubanƒÖ</i>. See also <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:schuiven.html>schuiven</a></i>, inherited from the same Proto-Germanic root. More at <span class="Latn" lang="en">shove</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:skat.html>skat</a> (67469)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_4">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From Germanic: cognate with Old Frisian skett ‚Äòmoney, cattle‚Äô, Old English sceatt, Dutch <a href = vnd.unilang:schat.html>schat</a>, Old High German scaz (German Schatz ‚Äòtreasure‚Äô), Old <a href = vnd.unilang:norse.html>Norse</a> skattr (Danish <i class="Latn mention" lang="da"><a href = vnd.unilang:skat.html>skat</a></i>, Icelandic <i class="Latn mention" lang="is">skattur</i>, Norwegian skatt), Gothic <span class="Goth" lang="got">êçÉêå∫êå∞êçÑêçÑêçÉ</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="got-Latn" class="tr Latn">skatts</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_5">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="osx"><a href = vnd.unilang:skat.html>skat</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span>

<ol><li>treasure, money, wealth</li>
<li>tax</li></ol>

<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Skelett</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">œÉŒ∫ŒµŒªŒµœÑœåœÇ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">skelet√≥s</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">‚Äú</span><span class="mention-gloss">dried up, withered, dried body, parched, mummy</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">‚Äù</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">œÉŒ∫ŒµŒªŒªœé</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">skell·πì</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">‚Äú</span><span class="mention-gloss">to dry, dry up, to make dry, to parch</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">‚Äù</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*(s)kelh‚ÇÅ-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">‚Äú</span><span class="mention-gloss">to parch, wither</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">‚Äù</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:skur.html>skur</a> (31585)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_4">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Swedish" class="extiw" title="w:Old Swedish">Old Swedish</a></span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Norse" class="extiw" title="w:Old Norse">Old <a href = vnd.unilang:norse.html>Norse</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="non">sk√∫r</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*sk≈´r≈ç</i>; cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Icelandic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Icelandic language">Icelandic</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="is">sk√∫r</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Schauer</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">schoer</i>, and <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">shower</i>, Old English <i>scur</i>, possibly relating to Latin <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">caurus</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="la-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">north-west wind</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<ol><li>a shower, a burst (of sudden rain, hail, arrows, bombs, electrons, curses, data transfer, etc.)

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> sl (12588)</h1><br></body> 
***sla.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:sla.html>sla</a> (918)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Originally the same word as <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:salade.html>salade</a></i> with reduction of the first syllable and regular loss of intervocalic <i>-d-</i> (compare <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:slee.html>slee</a></i> and <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:slede.html>slede</a></i>). The semantic distinction between both forms <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> secondary.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:sla.html>sla</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>uncountable</i>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:slaatje.html>slaatje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>lettuce</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">now especially diminutive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> salad
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:salade.html>salade</a></span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>

***slaan.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:slaan.html>slaan</a> (834)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">slaen</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">slƒÅn</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*slahanƒÖ</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_2">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:slaan.html>slaan</a></strong> 
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to hit, to <a href = vnd.unilang:slap.html>slap</a></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to beat, overcome</li>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:slagbal.html>slagbal</a> (99800)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Compound of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:slag.html>slag</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bal.html>bal</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:slagbal.html>slagbal</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>uncountable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>A sport similar to baseball and softball that <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> played on a <a href = vnd.unilang:smaller.html>smaller</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:according.html>according</a> to the official rules hexagonal, field with either a <a href = vnd.unilang:flat.html>flat</a> bat or a small cylindrical bat and in which <a href = vnd.unilang:runners.html>runners</a> receive an out when the ball <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> put on the home plate.</li></ol>

***slager.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:slager.html>slager</a> (6401)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:slager.html>slager</a></i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:slaan.html>slaan</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dictatoriaal.html>-er</a></i>. 
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:slager.html>slager</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:slagers.html>slagers</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:slager.html>slagertje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">butcher</span> <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">one who prepares and sells meat and meat products</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">killer</span>, slayer, murderer</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>In former times a <i><a href = vnd.unilang:slager.html>slager</a></i> would have also slaughtered animals, but in current language <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:slachter.html>slachter</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> used for that occupation, except for meat vendors who also operate their own slaughterhouses.

***slak.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:slak.html>slak</a> (13259)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">slecke</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">slacke</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <small>[Term?]</small>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*slikk≈ç</i>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Luxembourgish" class="extiw" title="w:Luxembourgish">Luxembourgish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="lb">Schleek</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Low German">Middle Low German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gml">slagge</i>, whence also <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Schlacke</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:slag.html>slag</a></i>. See the latter.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

</p>
<ol><li><a href = vnd.unilang:slag.html>slag</a> (the impurities which result and are separated out when melting a metal or refining it from its ore)</li>

***slang.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:slang.html>slang</a> (2647)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1_3">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">slange</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">slango</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*slang√¥</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">‚Äú</span><span class="mention-gloss">snake, serpent</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">‚Äù</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_8">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:slang.html>slang</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:slangen.html>slangen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:slangetje.html>slangetje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>snake, squamate of the suborder Serpentes
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl">serpent</span></span></dd>
<dd><span class="nyms hypernym"><span class="defdate">Hypernym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:reptiel.html>reptiel</a></span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li>hose <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">flexible tube</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>

***slangenmens.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:slangenmens.html>slangenmens</a> (43063)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Compound of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:slang.html>slang</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">‚Äú</span><span class="mention-gloss">snake</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">‚Äù</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-en-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="ann-pos">interfix</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:mens.html>mens</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">‚Äú</span><span class="mention-gloss">human</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">‚Äù</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. First used in 1880 as the artist name of one Charles <a href = vnd.unilang:michel.html>Michel</a>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:slangenmens.html>slangenmens</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> or <abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:slangenmensen.html>slangenmensen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:slangenmens.html>slangenmensje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">contortionist</span> <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">acrobat whose body can be contorted into unusual postures</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<ul><li><b>1880</b> December 2, "1 eenige <a href = vnd.unilang:buitengewone.html>buitengewone</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:voorstelling.html>voorstelling</a>" (advertisement), Vlissingse <a href = vnd.unilang:courant.html>Courant</a>, page 4.
<dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>Het</a> <b>slangenmensch</b><br /><a href = vnd.unilang:door.html>door</a> Charles <a href = vnd.unilang:michel.html>Michel</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:uit.html>uit</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:parijs.html>Parijs</a>.</span><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">The <b>contortionist</b>, [performed] by Charles <a href = vnd.unilang:michel.html>Michel</a> from Paris.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:slaper.html>slaper</a> (26934)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:slaper.html>slaper</a></i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:slapen.html>slapen</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dictatoriaal.html>-er</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:slaper.html>slaper</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:slapers.html>slapers</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:slaper.html>slapertje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>, <i>feminine</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">slaapster</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A sleeper, one who <a href = vnd.unilang:sleeps.html>sleeps</a>.</li>
<li>A dyke that doesn'<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a> function as a water barrier but <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> capable of acting as a reserve barrier.
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl">slaperdijk</span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>
